Jinting Guild Hall and Piaomiao Society 133

The Jinting Guild Hall, located on Lujiabang in the Nanshi district of this city, was established by natives of Xishan, Dongting who were living in Shanghai. It has been around for several decades and has approximately 2,000 members. The guild hall building was also built with donations from the natives. Unexpectedly, recently a native named Zheng Zhuping suddenly initiated the Piaomiao Society, whose purpose is no different from that of a native-place association. For a time, more than a hundred people joined the society, and a founding convention was held on the 15th of this month. During the meeting, executive and supervisory committee members were elected by ballot. However, because the election results were unfavorable, they caused opposition from the members, who petitioned the city's Party headquarters to send someone to recount the votes. Yesterday, the recount revealed that the number of votes did not match the list of elected individuals. It is said that some natives who are not members of the society have telegraphed their opposition to the society and sent a letter to the Jinting Guild Hall to inquire: given that the society and the guild hall have the same purpose, where should the natives turn to in the future? This is based on the principle that two organizations of the same nature should not be established in the same area. After receiving the letter, the guild hall has submitted the situation to the city's Party headquarters for clarification.

National Bibliography of Life Published 139

Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau Announces Simple Life Insurance Regulations: Individuals and Groups Can Pay Premiums and Take Out Insurance According to Regulations, Divided into Whole Life Insurance and Term Life Insurance 140

The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau will handle simple life insurance and will begin operations in Shanghai and Nanjing on the 2nd of next month, and in Hankou on the 10th.

Insurance Regulations have been approved and promulgated by the National Government. Chapter 1: General Provisions. Article 1: All life insurance policies with a value between 50 yuan and 500 yuan, whether they are individual or group contracts, fall within the scope of simple life insurance. Article 2: Simple life insurance is supervised and managed by the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, which also guides the handling of various postal savings and remittance sub-bureaus and post offices. Article 3: Simple life insurance is divided into whole life insurance and term life insurance. Two types, term life insurance is further divided into the following four types: (1) 10-year term life insurance, (2) 15-year term life insurance, (3) 20-year term life insurance, (4) 25-year term life insurance. Article 4: The premium rates for various insurance contracts in the preceding article are calculated at a weekly interest rate of 3.5%, according to the specified mortality table. Article 5: The Insurance Bureau has the right to choose risks. If the occupation of the insured is deemed excessively dangerous, or the physical condition is deemed weak, the Insurance Bureau may refuse insurance. Article 6: The Insurance Bureau may request the policyholder or beneficiary to provide a guarantee if it deems it necessary for the responsibilities assumed by the policyholder in the insurance contract and the matters stated. Article 7: After the establishment of the insurance contract, all documents delivered to the Insurance Bureau regarding insurance contract matters must specify the symbol and number of the insurance policy, and a receipt must be obtained upon delivery. Article 8: If the insurance policy, premium receipt, payment voucher, or loan receipt is lost or damaged and cannot be reused, the policyholder or beneficiary may request a reissue or replacement of a copy. For requesting a reissue or replacement of an insurance policy or premium receipt, a handling fee of 2 jiao of silver per item must be paid. Article 9: When requesting a reissue or replacement of a copy, an application form must be filled out in the prescribed format, and the required handling fee must be paid by purchasing postage stamps and affixing them to the application form, which must be delivered to the Insurance Bureau together. If it is a request to replace the original, the original must also be returned. If a copy is issued by the Insurance Bureau, the original will be invalid. Article 10: When there are several policyholders or beneficiaries in the same insurance contract, one person should be mutually elected as a representative, who has full agency authority. If there are several policyholders in an insurance contract and a representative is elected, the responsibility that they should bear is still borne jointly by all policyholders.

Establishment of the Contract Chapter 2: Establishment of the Contract. Article 11: When making an offer, the policyholder should truthfully fill in the insurance application form with the following items, and deliver it together with the first premium to the Insurance Bureau or its dispatched premium collector, and request a temporary premium receipt: (1) Type of insurance; (2) Amount of premium and method of paying the premium during the insurance period (paying to the Insurance Bureau or the premium collector); (3) Amount of insurance; (4) Name and address of the policyholder; (5) In the event of Article 10, the name of the agent; (6) Name, date of birth (year, month, and day), occupation, and address of the insured; (7) Name of the beneficiary and their relationship with the insured; (8) What diseases the insured has had or currently has, stating the name of the disease and its course; (9) If the insured has previously taken out simple life insurance, the remaining amount insured, and the symbol and number of the insurance policy. If an offer to take out insurance has been made but not approved, the situation regarding the offer and the amount to be insured should be recorded together (10) If it is desired to pay the insurance premium and the insurance premium of other contracts at the same time, a statement should be attached, and the symbol and number of each insurance policy should be recorded together with the payment date specified in Article 21. When the insured of the insurance contract is a third party other than the beneficiary, the offer in the preceding paragraph should first obtain their consent, and their name should be signed and stamped on the application form. Article 12: When making an offer, the policyholder should invite the insured to meet at the Bureau. Article 13: According to the provisions of the preceding article, if the insured happens to be in another place, making it impossible for the Insurance Bureau to meet with them, the insured may meet with the Insurance Bureau at their location. In the event of the situation in the preceding paragraph, the policyholder should fill in the detailed address of the insured on the insurance application form. Article 14: Once an offer to take out insurance is approved and the first premium is paid, the insurer should immediately fill out and issue an insurance policy and a premium receipt. When the offer in the preceding paragraph is rejected by the insurer, the policyholder should be notified immediately to hold the temporary premium receipt and go to the Insurance Bureau to recover the premium paid. Article 15: The insurance policy should record the following items, and be signed and stamped by the Director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau: (1) Type of insurance; (2) Amount of insurance; (3) Amount of premium and insurance period; (4) Name of the policyholder, insured, and beneficiary: and the insured's date of birth (year, month, and day) (5) Date of filling out the insurance policy, and the symbol and number of the policy (5) Date of expiry of the insurance contract (in the case of term life insurance) The method of translating it into French, German, Russian, Italian, Japanese or Esperanto, all indicate the name of the original author and the original title of the book. All original book titles that cannot be found in various translated books and bibliographies can be found in this bibliography. If there are printing errors in the original book or errors in the business bibliography, they will all be corrected one by one. If a book has several editions, they are arranged in one place, which is very convenient for purchasing books and compiling catalogs. Readers at all levels add symbols according to the depth of the content. (4) Convenient inspection: There are four types of indexes: classification index, subject index, continent and country index, and foreign author index. Any book can be found with one search. With this book, it can serve as the most reliable guide for purchasing books, selecting books, classifying books, and cataloging books. It is really a reference book that all readers, libraries, schools, cultural institutions, and families must have. The hardcover book costs only 4 jiao, with postage added for other places.

A Visit to the China Wool Textile Factory (Continued) 144

— Wu Yuxuan

The second part of the factory is the wool dyeing field. It is to dye the bundled wool threads into various colors for buyers to choose from. The dyeing site of the factory can be divided into two major processes: dyeing and air drying. In the dyeing part, there are four automatic dyeing machines. The so-called automatic dyeing machine uses a pump to circulate the boiling water in the dyeing tank, so as to avoid the disadvantage of uneven dye paste when the velvet thread is dyed. In addition, there are two manual dyeing machines for emergency needs. Now these four automatic dyeing machines can dye 56 different colors. After the wool thread is dyed, the second step is to send it to a hot air dryer for air drying. An electric fan is installed on the machine, and a water tank is installed below. Usually the temperature inside the machine is often 70 degrees Celsius. The dyed wool thread is sent into the machine and can be blown dry in 20 minutes.

The last part is the inspection and packaging area of ​​the wool thread. The dyed wool thread must undergo manual inspection to see if there are any defects. If it is considered perfect after inspection, the trademark is manually pasted and packed, so as to prepare for transportation to the central market to serve. So far, the manufacturing work of wool threads is all completed.

The factory currently has more than 100 male and female workers, most of whom are female workers. The factory treats workers not only by paying wages according to their working ability, but also by providing food and accommodation to reduce the trivialities of the daily life of the workers so that they can work with peace of mind. At the same time, special attention is paid to the management and training of male and female workers. Because workers are a major element of production, the knowledge, skills, and health of workers are closely related to production capacity. Therefore, the factory should also conduct special training based on the above three principles in addition to the workers' work. The factory's production capacity can now spin 1,800 pounds of wool thread per day, and the highest can reach more than 2,000 pounds. The products it produces are divided into knitted cashmere (i.e. knitted wool thread) and hand-woven cashmere (hand-woven wool thread), both of which are of excellent quality. Knitted cashmere is mostly 40-count and 32-count thread, and hand-woven cashmere is mostly 4-strand thread. The daily production of knitted and hand-woven cashmere is about 900 pounds each. The trademark used when selling it on the mountain market is the Foreign Queen brand, which means that it has the ambition to expand the world market.

After the visit, the reporters were very pleased, but I personally felt that there was still one thing that must be improved, that is, the issue of raw material use. The raw materials currently used in the factory are wool tops rather than raw wool. Most of these wool tops are purchased from Australia, and occasionally from countries such as England and France, but domestic products have not yet been adopted. According to Mr. Chen, the factory's reason for using foreign wool tops is that China's customs charges the same tax rate for imports of wool tops and raw wool. However, when manufacturing wool threads, the wool threads that can be made from raw wool are only about half of the wool threads made from the same amount of wool tops. For the sake of overall cost, it is not necessary to purchase Sichuan wool as raw materials. As for domestic wool, due to the quality of the wool thread, only Shanxi Province has an annual production of about 60,000 pounds that can be used by the factory, while the factory needs more than 2 million pounds of wool per year, which is far from meeting the demand. But in my memory, northern China is rich in wool. The annual export volume is quite large. Taking last year as an example, China's wool exports were more than 250,000 dan, worth more than 34 million yuan. If the factory can study and improve the manufacturing method and find ways to use domestic wool, then the factory's raw materials will not be controlled by foreigners in the future, and its future development will be even more unlimited.

Radio Weekly of Shen Bao

The Influence of Constellations on Radio Waves 145

— Jueming

(1) The Relationship Between Constellations and Radio Waves

Anyone who has studied radio even slightly knows how closely radio waves are related to the sun and moon, especially the number of sunspots, solar eclipses, and the position of the moon, which have the greatest impact on radio waves.

However, relatively few people pay attention to the stars that fill the sky like so many pearls and gemstones. Ordinary radio researchers may think that the stars are too small to be of any importance and therefore can be ignored. But this is a big mistake. If we think about how many constellations are around the earth, it is not difficult to know how great their impact on radio waves is. What's more, the sun and moon, strictly speaking, are just one of the constellations.

For the sake of convenience, the stars are divided into "meteors" and "constellations" and explained in detail below:

(2) The Relationship Between Meteors and Radio Waves

On a clear evening sky, when looking up at the bright moon or counting those brilliant stars, you can often see a streak of starlight flying by, as if the stars are moving house. This is the so-called "meteor."

In astronomy, meteors have no direct relationship with fixed stars. Meteors are actually fragments of iron or stone floating and wandering between constellations, which are attracted by the earth's gravity and run into the earth's atmosphere, colliding and rubbing against the air to generate high heat and light.

According to scholars' analysis, the main components of meteors are no more than: light gas, oxygen, nitrogen, carbon, magnesium, sodium, iron, copper, aluminum, calcium, manganese, nickel, silicon, potassium, cobalt, etc. These substances become tiny powder scattered in the air, its size is about one-tenth or one-hundredth of a micron in diameter (i.e. one millionth of a meter.) This kind of fine particles stays in the air for a long time and is not easy to fall. According to the research of Dr. Nagaoka in Japan, it takes about three years for the place where the meteor occurs to reach the surface of the earth. Ordinary meteors occur on average at a height of 114.4 zai from the earth's surface and disappear at 79.6 zai; however, there are also some that reach the earth's surface, but the number is very small. Its falling speed is about 4.40 meters per second.

The "Icn" generated by this kind of meteor diffuses around the meteor's orbit. The disappearance of this "Icn" varies depending on its diffusion state, the impact of the Earth's magnetic force, and the light pressure of sunlight, so it cannot be generalized, but generally speaking, it seems to take a lot of time; the impact of meteors on radio waves often continues to exist for dozens of days, which is why.

So how many of these meteors are there? According to astronomers, there are about eight visible to the naked eye per hour; however, what we can see in our eyes, in other words, our visual field, is actually only a small part of the sky around the earth. In fact, the total number of meteors that can be seen by the naked eye of all mankind on earth is about more than 20 million per day; if we include those that cannot be seen by the naked eye and must be observed with a telescope, then the number is as high as 400 million. From this point of view, the great influence of meteors on radio waves is not without reason.

Not only that, there is a so-called "meteor swarm" in the orbit that the earth is traveling in; in this orbit, meteor streams are scattered in groups, the number is the most; so when the earth enters this orbit, the influence of the meteor stream on radio waves will naturally be the most intense. (To be continued)

Ultra-Short Wave Emission Vacuum Tube 146

— Pao

No. 304A

The progress of radio science has promoted the increase of countless radio stations, and the current frequency range is not enough to be allocated. Therefore, the ultra-short wave band with a vast land and sparse population has been gradually developed. In order to conduct further research on ultra-short waves, ultra-short wave emission vacuum tubes that can generate greater power are of course in great need.

Ordinary emission vacuum tubes can still work normally at a frequency of about 15 MHz (20 meters); but above 30 MHz, the efficiency is greatly reduced; when the frequency is higher, there is even no output. According to research results, the reason why the effectiveness of emission vacuum tubes weakens at extremely high frequencies is probably: 1. The current that charges the interelectrode capacitance of the vacuum tube increases due to the increased frequency, and this current passes through the wires inside the tube, resulting in extremely large power loss. 2. When the frequency increases, the oscillation period (Pariod) is similar to the time required for electrons to travel from the cathode to the screen, and the thunder voltage current in each part is in an inappropriate phase (such as the screen voltage and screen current), and the output is small. 3. At extremely high frequencies, the self-inductance and capacitance in the matching circuit are very small. Therefore, the internal self-inductance and capacitance of the vacuum tube, which can usually be ignored, also have a great impact at this time. Therefore, vacuum tubes for generating ultra-short waves must: thicken the wires inside the tube, reduce the distance between the screen cathode appropriately, and reduce the internal self-inductance and capacitance to the minimum possible range. The 304A (Westerne'ectric 304A) ultra-short wave emission vacuum tube of the Western Electric Company of the United States is designed and manufactured based on the above-mentioned improvements.

The external shape of 304A is shown in the attached figure. Its grid and screen are led out from the top of the glass tube (therefore the lead wire is shortened, and the support for the grid or screen can be omitted. Moreover, the insulation ability of glass at extremely high frequencies is also excellent). The screen is made of graphite (graphite has a higher heat dissipation capacity than metal, so the screen area is reduced and the interelectrode capacitance is also reduced at the same time): the screen is very close to the cathode, so the time for electrons to fly from the cathode to the screen is also considerably reduced. 304A is used for oscillation and amplification. At 100 MHz (3 meters), it can work according to the specified power (output about 110 watts at a screen voltage of 1,250 volts); if the frequency is higher, the output will be reduced considerably, but it can still have considerable output at 300 MHz (1 meter!).

Electrical Power and Electrical Rate (Continued) 147

— En Lun

The quantity marked within the semicircle in the diagram equals the product of the quantities marked within the two quadrants multiplied together; the quantity marked within one quadrant equals the quotient of the quantity marked within the semicircle divided by the quantity marked within the other quadrant.

According to Ohm's Law, electrical power can also be expressed in terms of current and resistance, or voltage and resistance. Because V=IR

Therefore P=VI=IRXI=I2R……(4)

Because I=VR

Therefore P=VI=VXVV2……(5)＝RR

Electrical power is the product of voltage and current. Therefore, if there is voltage but no current, or if there is current but no voltage, the electrical power is equal to zero. The diagram above shows the relationship between the output electrical power (Output Power) of a generator or battery and the change in load resistance (Load resistance). Ammeter A and voltmeter V are connected to measure the electrical power output.

(A) The diagram shows an open circuit (Opon Circuit) in the output circuit, where the line resistance is infinite. Therefore, the current measured by the ammeter is zero. Although the voltage measured by the voltmeter is the full value of the generated voltage, the electrical power is the product of the output current and output voltage, so the output electrical power is also equal to zero. (B) The diagram shows that the output circuit has no resistance, called a short circuit (Short Circuit), so the current measured by the ammeter is extremely high. However, because the resistance of the output circuit is zero, the voltage measured by the voltmeter is zero. Therefore, the output electrical power is also zero; all the electrical power of the generator is consumed by the internal resistance of the machine itself. (C) The diagram shows a normal output circuit, where the circuit resistance is R. If R is varied, the current and voltage will change accordingly, so the output electrical power will also change. As the resistance increases, the current decreases, but the voltage increases; conversely, as the resistance decreases, the current increases, but the voltage decreases. The electrical power output is maximized when R is exactly equal to the internal resistance of the machine.

Electrical work is the product of electrical power and time. Let T represent time, and W represent electrical work, then W=VIF…………(6)

W=I2RF……(7)

Or W=V2FR……(8)

When time is measured in seconds, the unit of electrical work or electrical energy is the Joule; a Joule is the electrical energy consumed by a current of I Ampere flowing through a resistance of I Ohm in I second, or the work done by a current of one Ampere at a voltage of one Volt in one second. In formulas (6), (7), and (8), if V is in Volts, I is in Amperes, R is in Ohms, and T is in seconds, then W is in Joules. Therefore,

Joule = Volts × Amperes × Seconds

Watt = Joules/Second

When time is measured in hours, the unit of electrical work is the Watt-hour; one Watt-hour is the product of one Watt of electrical power and one hour. Larger units of electrical work include hectowatt-hours and kilowatt-hours. The electricity measured by ordinary electric meters (commonly called "fire meters") is in kilowatt-hours. One "unit of electricity" is one kilowatt-hour. (To be continued)

Longhua Round Trip Long-Distance Run to be Held Tomorrow Morning; Route Map Published Yesterday; Total Distance of Twelve Miles; List of 215 Athletes and Numbers Announced 154

The third Longhua round-trip long-distance run, organized by the Xiguang Cross-Country Team, has been in preparation for a long time and is now scheduled to start tomorrow morning at 8:00 AM in front of the Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road in Nanshi, with Shen Yuguang firing the starting gun. There will be a total of 215 participants. The total distance is 11 English miles. The chief referee is Jiang Lianggui, the timing chief is Han Kuiyong, the general commander is Xia Kaiming, and the chief recorder is Wu Zhenqing. Other officials have been mentioned in previous reports and will be omitted. The full route and precautions announced by the team yesterday are recorded below:

Precautions

Due to the excessive distance, although there will be Boy Scouts taking care of the athletes along the way, the team is concerned that unexpected events may occur to the athletes along the way. Therefore, athletes can bring one escort to take care of them along the way by bicycle, to provide route guidance and supply drinks. This is extremely important, and the team hopes that all athletes will pay attention. Athletes can collect their bib numbers from the preparation director, Wu Zhenqing, before the race. All officials will follow behind in cars and motorcycles provided by the association.

Full Route

Start in front of the Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road in Nanshi, enter Daxing Street through Xiaoximen, then Lujiabang, cross Xieqiao Zhizaoju Road, pass Shanghai Girls' High School, turn right onto Xietu Road, then onto Lushan Road, then turn left onto Kangqu Road to Shaorihui Bridge, Nanyang Middle School, the Shanghai Garrison Headquarters, and go straight to Chenjiawan, 1,000 meters south of the Longhua Pagoda (there is a mile marker No. 208 on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway at this location), then return to the original site on Zhonghua Road by the same route. The entire distance is 11 miles, approximately 20,000 meters, or 36 li.

Middle School Ball Games Begin on the 4th; Divided into Men's and Women's Basketball, Volleyball, Soccer, and Ping Pong; 11 Schools Participating in Men's, 9 in Women's 155

The second meeting of the preparatory committee for the Shanghai Middle School Ball Games was held at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday at the Great Education Association of the Chinese Arts and Sciences Society. All ball games are scheduled to begin on December 4 and end on the 31st. Men's are divided into three events: basketball, volleyball, and small soccer, with 11 participating schools. Women's are divided into three events: basketball, volleyball, and table tennis, with 9 participating schools. Details are as follows:

Preparatory Meeting Resolutions: The second preparatory meeting was attended by Han Juemin and Pan Chengbin from Pudong Middle School; Cheng Keyou and Wu Chenglie from Kaiming Middle School; Wu Zhiqian and Huang Shengbai from Shanghai Girls' High School; and Tong Hangbai and Lai Zhiwen from Minli Girls' Middle School. Chairman: Han Juefa. Secretary: Pan Chengbin. Key resolutions: (1) The opening date is set from the 4th to the 31st of next month. (2) Divided into men's and women's groups. The schools participating in men's basketball are Guoguang, Kaiming, Yuqing, Zhengfeng, Pudong, Quanzhang, Qingnian, Xinhuan, Zhengshi, and Guangxia. Participating in volleyball are Qingnian, Zhengshi, and Pudong. Participating in small soccer are Yuqing, Pudong, Xinhuan, Zhengshi, and Private Shanghai Middle School. The schools participating in women's basketball are Huadong, Biwen, Shanghai Girls' High School, Daozhong, Xinhuan, Guangxia, and Shanghai Kindergarten Normal School. Participating in volleyball are Minli, China, Shanghai Girls' High School, Huadong, Shanghai Kindergarten Normal School, and Biwen. Participating in table tennis are Huadong, Shanghai Girls' High School, and Daozhong. (3) Task assignments: Kaiming and Minli are responsible for the refereeing group; Pudong and Shanghai Girls' High School are responsible for the scheduling group; Zhengshi is responsible for the administrative group; the principals of the five schools are responsible for the review committee; and the sports directors of the five schools are responsible for the referee committee. (4) Schools that have not submitted team photos must submit them to the original registration location before the 3rd of next month. (5) School fees must be paid to Huang Shengbai at Shanghai Girls' High School before the start of the games. (6) Only students who are currently enrolled in the school are allowed to participate in the games. Otherwise, the qualification of the school to participate in the games will be cancelled upon investigation by the review committee. (7) The regulations for each ball game are as follows:

Competition Regulations: Shanghai Middle School Ball Games Regulations (1) Dates: From December 4 to December 31, starting at 3:30 PM every day, and at 9:00 AM on Sunday mornings. Failure to arrive within 15 minutes will be considered a forfeit. In case of an accident, the reasons must be stated for consideration and handling. (2) Locations: The games will be played in rotation at nearby school ball courts that meet the standards, or at the Shanghai Municipal Stadium. (3) Method: All ball games will use a single round-robin system. (4) Rules: Based on the latest published rules of the China National Sports Federation, except for small soccer, which will be based on the rules published by the Shanghai Municipal Stadium. (5) Referees: The refereeing group will appoint referees based on the actual situation. (6) Scoring: Each victory earns two points, a draw earns one point for each team, and a loss earns zero points. The team with the most points at the end wins the championship. In the event that two or more teams have the same score, the refereeing group will schedule a rematch to determine the winner. (7) Ball: Each school will provide its own national standard ball for the games. The referee will choose which ball to use during the game. (8) Uniforms: Each school must have a uniform color, and the uniform must have clear numbers. (9) School team line-ups cannot be changed once the competition has started. (10) Photos: Photos must be verified before the start of the game before entry is permitted. If there is a mismatch, the team's qualification will be cancelled. (11) Once the location and time of the game are announced, they cannot be changed. In case of special circumstances, the refereeing group must determine that there is a legitimate reason before accommodation is permitted. (12) Postponement: If the weather is rainy or the field is too wet to play, the refereeing group will determine another date for a make-up game. If there is a special event, it must be agreed upon with the other party before a reschedule can be made. (13) Fees: Schools participating in one event must pay a fee of $1.50, schools participating in two events must pay a fee of $3.00, and so on. (14) Awards: In addition to trophies, all participating schools will receive souvenirs. (15) Protests: If there is a protest, it must be submitted in writing to the review committee after the event, along with a protest fee of five silver dollars. The fee will be returned if the protest is upheld after review, otherwise it will be used as a fee. (16) The office is temporarily located at the Shanghai Municipal Education Association on Daji Road. (17) The preparatory committee may modify these regulations at any time if there are any shortcomings.

Basketball Match: Guoguang Team Defeats Seven Teams Yesterday; Seven Teams' Veterans Lead by Two Points in the First Half; Guoguang's Fierce Comeback in the Second Half Leads to Victory 157

The Guoguang Middle School basketball team members, though once defeated by Youyou, are quite strong, excelling in both offense and defense, not comparable to ordinary middle school basketball teams. This year, they also added Xiqing. In preparation for vigorous training, they specially invited seven basketball teams for a friendly match at the Youyou basketball court yesterday. The seven teams were all veteran players, but having been away from the court for a long time, they lacked stamina and had difficulty running. They had a fierce presence upon entering the court. Wang Huating took advantage of Chen Anbang's foul to score first, and Guoguang's Gao Baosheng immediately responded. From then on, both sides made progress, and the scores were very close. Guoguang eventually fell behind. In the first half, the seven teams led with a score of thirteen to eleven. Starting from the second half, the veterans became fatigued, while Guoguang became increasingly adept at playing, and their shooting was particularly accurate, although there were occasional mistakes in their movements, which was a slight flaw. As a result, Guoguang made a comeback with a score of twenty-seven to twenty-four. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

Educational News

Education Ministry Inspector Zhong Visits: Zhejiang Province Vocational Education Report (4) 162

Fifteen, Provincial Obstetric School and Private Jisheng Obstetric School

The Provincial Obstetric School currently has two classes with 50 students. They are recommended by various counties, which are responsible for their expenses. After graduation, they return to their original places of origin to set up obstetric clinics. The intention is excellent, but the students are young, averaging less than 18 years old, which has a significant impact on their service beliefs. The equipment of the affiliated hospital is being improved and is considered complete. The original regulations allowed for graduation after two years, followed by three to four months of internship before being assigned. This should be changed to comply with the new regulations, with a uniform three-year program, increasing the internship period for proficiency.

The Private Jisheng Obstetric School has two classes with 35 students. The hospital and all equipment are rudimentary, and there are very few maternity patients hospitalized, so students cannot gain practical experience. After graduation, they visit the Provincial Hospital for several weeks and then undergo three months of internship. The methods and regulations do not comply with the requirements. In general, the school is quite capable of technical cooperation with the Provincial Hospital, but the lack of resources is a significant inconvenience and should be improved.

Sixteen, Private Zhijiang College Affiliated High School Business Department, Private Jishan High School Senior Business Department

The Business Department of the Private Zhijiang Affiliated High School was newly established this year and currently has only one class with 25 students. The main purpose is to prepare students for admission to the school's economics department. The method is not ideal. General courses account for 25 hours per week and are taught in the same classes as regular middle school students. Business courses include only commercial geography, bookkeeping, abacus calculation, and an overview of commerce, totaling ten hours, which does not comply with the regulations. There is no practical training equipment. It should be improved quickly. Business courses should account for five-eighths of the total curriculum, with the remainder focusing on preparing for employment.

The Business Department of Private Jishan High School has three classes with 50 students. The first graduating class this year saw approximately half of its students find employment. The school's bank is relatively well-established, while the store is very simple, with three typewriters. The allocation of practice time is appropriate. Most of the general courses are taught in the same classes as the regular department. There are nine banks in the school's location. Efforts should be made to strengthen connections and cooperation to seek convenience. There is still a lack of attention to the practical problems of business and the province's production and consumption situation.

Seventeen, Ningbo County Vocational Commercial School, Zhenhai County Junior Commercial School, Jiaxing County Junior Commercial School, Haining County Junior Middle School Junior Commercial Department

Ningbo County Vocational Commercial School is divided into junior and senior levels, with six junior commercial classes and three senior commercial classes, totaling 340 students. The junior commercial program is divided into two-year and three-year systems. The former is designed for those who hope to complete their studies quickly for employment purposes. The content of the academic and commercial subjects is less and simpler compared to the three-year system. The senior level has a banking department. The junior commercial level has practical training in stores, typing, bookkeeping, and abacus calculation. The store organization is quite complete, which is rare in other schools. However, daily business is limited, with sales limited to stationery and food. The amount of money coming in and out is very small, and the value of the training materials is very low. If it can be expanded to outside the school, increase capital, and improve business, this kind of organization will be more beneficial. The school bank for senior students' practice, although the procedures and methods are the same as actual banks, the small amount of money involved may prevent students from taking things seriously. Every effort should be made to entrust the collection of tuition and meal fees and encourage teachers and students to deposit money to expand the scope. About half of the junior commercial graduates find employment, mostly in banks, with a few continuing their studies. Management is lax, and there is no training in good commercial habits. If adapting to environmental needs is considered, commercial supplementary classes should be added.

Zhenhai County Junior Commercial School has four classes with about 100 students. The practical training equipment is very simple, and teaching also lacks practicality. The first graduating class this year faces great difficulty in finding employment. Most of them continue their studies in senior commercial schools. If the school can contact business magnates beforehand, it seems that there should not be a problem to introduce the dozen or so students. The school's difficulty in student placement and a small number of local people advocate restoring junior high school, and the matter is being submitted for approval. This is not a good solution. In terms of the environment, Zhenhai merchants hold the leading position in Shanghai's business community and should be a suitable place for running junior commercial schools or commercial supplementary classes. The school should invite business leaders to organize advisory or placement committees to plan for student placement in advance to avoid temporary panic and helplessness.

Jiaxing County Junior Commercial School has three classes, with the third grade divided into typing and bookkeeping groups, totaling over 100 students. Although it has a long history, its performance is ordinary. Only half of the graduates engage in commerce. The typing and bookkeeping equipment is still good, but the bank and stores are very simple. Most of the students are children of businessmen. The teaching of various subjects, such as commercial geography and commercial arithmetic, lacks relevance and is not suitable for the times. Commercial supplementary classes should be added or redesigned to accommodate students who are employed part-time.

Haining County Junior Middle School Commercial Department is similar to Jiaxing County Junior Commercial School, with one class of 40 students. Most students, except for those who are employed part-time, have no commercial prospects. The practical training equipment is extremely lacking. There are many general subjects, focusing on preparing for further studies. Methods should be found to improve this. If necessary, commercial supplementary classes should be established.

Ministry of Education Explains: Elementary School Teacher Certification Issues 164

The Ministry of Education recently instructed the Jiangsu Education Department to respond to a request from the Jurong County Education Bureau for instructions on whether teachers who have studied at the Provincial Normal School for two years and served for more than two years can be granted non-examination certification in accordance with regulations. The instruction stated that elementary school teachers who have studied at the old-system normal school for three years or the high school normal department for two years and served for more than two years can be granted non-examination certification in accordance with the provisions of Article 5, Paragraph 1 of the Provisional Regulations for Elementary School Teacher Certification. You are hereby informed and instructed to inform accordingly.

Temple Property Appropriated for Education Funding Cannot Be Reclaimed on Pretext: All Temples Should Fulfill Registration: Municipal Government Ordered by Higher Authority to Instruct the Social Affairs Bureau to Handle 167

The Executive Yuan stated that after the promulgation and implementation of the Regulations on the Supervision of Temples, all temple properties that have been appropriated for education funding by provincial and municipal governments should not be reclaimed and should maintain the status quo. Regarding urging provincial and municipal governments to implement temple registration in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Regulations on the Supervision of Temples, the Ministry of Interior should expedite the handling. As for the funds for temples to run public welfare undertakings, emphasis should be placed on expanding local education undertakings, which should be implemented conscientiously by provincial and municipal governments. Therefore, the Executive Yuan specially instructed the Municipal Government to comply. The Municipal Government yesterday ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to comply swiftly.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (110) 170

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"Yes, Mei and Nan will take good care of you, but you must all be back at the gate at five o'clock, and the steward will come to pick you up."

Robert, grateful, threw himself into his mother's arms, promising to bring her back every blackberry he had picked and not eat a single one himself. So the children all piled into the hay wagon and rattled away, and the happiest face among that dozen children, needless to say, was Robert's. He sat between his two temporary little mothers, waving his best hat and smiling cheerfully at the whole world.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 171

— (Lan Shan)

Everyone pays respect and sings praises to the victors. Where is there time to comfort a victimized lamb? The plaintive weeping of the weak and small drifts in the cold wind of the night. How can it compare to the pleasing sound of a triumphal song?

We humans live in hope and perish in despair.

A smile through tears is more sorrowful than mournful cries.

A child struggling in a warm bed is the first step of resistance.

Our life force should be like a clock that tells time accurately, step by step, never stopping, doing what needs to be done without a second of error.

A friend said with emotion, "Only death can reveal true love. Where has true love ever existed in the world?" Another said, "To seek true love in this world is better than seeking sympathy in hell." Both are insightful views, but those who are lost in the sea of love and desire will not awaken.

In Memory of Mr. Sun Deqian 172

— Ping Chang

I was traveling in Japan when Mr. Sun Deqian passed away. I only learned of it upon my return to the country, from Professor Ma Gongyu. I sighed for several days. Mr. Sun, known as Aikang, was from Wuxian. He was knowledgeable in all fields of study, especially proficient in the works of various philosophers. He was of noble character and indifferent to worldly fame. He taught at the Shanghai University in his old age and lived in poverty. He passed away at the end of last month due to stomach illness at the age of sixty-nine. His published works include over twenty books such as "Critical Analysis of Sima Qian's Historical Records," "Examples of Bibliography in the Book of Han," and "General Outline of Ancient Books on Various Philosophers," which are profound and comprehensive, unprecedented. Scholars in Japan admired him greatly. During the reign of Emperor Showa, Minister of Education Etō Chizuru presented his book for imperial review. According to the Japanese, such an honor is not easily obtained even by natives. At that time, Wu Changshuo jokingly said to Mr. Sun, "I received a bronze statue, only from calligraphy and painting friends. It is a small matter going from below to above. You can be called a gentleman going from above to above." I once read a Japanese cultural publication that called Zhang Taiyan a great writer, but called Mr. Sun a great scholar. In fact, Mr. Sun's writing is compared with Li Shenyan. Qian Jibo once said, "In modern times, these two are the only masters of parallel prose." Wang Guowei said that Shenyan was too ornate, while Mr. Sun's style was free and clear, so he should be superior. Wang Guowei did not praise people lightly, but he admired Mr. Sun and Zhang Mengqu. He once visited Shen Meisou with them. Meisou gave them a poem with the line, "Three guests gather at Wuhui at one time, and ninety percent of the people doubt it," referring to Mr. Sun, Wang Guowei, and Zhang Mengqu. Meisou also once said, "There are many poets and few writers in Shanghai, many writers and few scholars. You and Wang and Zhang are truly worthy of being scholars." These are all things I learned from being by the side of the elders in the past. It has not been long since Meisou returned to the mountain, and Wang Guowei drowned himself. Now, Mr. Sun's death has also been heard. The great masters of national studies have almost all withered away, and the fate of the nation is even more unbearable to ask. Alas, how can I not mourn in my heart! (No payment accepted)

Idle Talk in Rongcheng 173

— Jia Chengsheng

Opium smoke is like chronic tuberculosis, harming life and destroying nature, with extreme consequences. Yet those who are addicted to it think it can provide momentary excitement, so they do not hesitate to drink poison to quench their thirst. Now its poison has spread throughout the country, posing a great obstacle to the future of the nation. The government has issued strict orders and severe prohibitions to save the country from danger, which is well-founded.

The name of opium varies. It is called Wuxiang, or Wuyan. Its original name is opium, also called Apian, also called Yarong, also called Afurong, also called Hepurong.

China originally did not produce this substance. It was imported from foreign countries. However, from what time and from where it was imported is unknown. In historical records, the "Great Ming Code" records tribute from various countries, stating that opium was included in the tribute from countries such as Siam and Java. This is the earliest record. The import of opium may have begun at this time.

Also, in the "Compendium of Materia Medica" written by Li Shizhen during the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty, the "Grain" section says: Opium was rarely heard of in previous generations, but recently some have used it. It also says: Afurong is the sap of the poppy flower. When the bud is forming, use a needle to prick the outer green skin in the afternoon, being careful not to damage the inner skin. Prick three to five places. The next morning, the sap will come out. Scrape it into porcelain with a bamboo knife and dry it in the shade for medicinal use.

Also, Fang Yizhi's "Minor Knowledge of Physics" says: Collect the sap of poppies into porcelain, seal the mouth with paper, and use it after sunning it for fourteen days. The method has been passed down like this. It is used to treat diarrhea or as a bedroom medicine. It is warm and astringent and not very harmful. This is all used as medicine. If it is loaded into a gun and inhaled, there is no such method.

I remember that someone once wrote a pagoda poem about opium smoke, which was extremely humorous. The poem says: "Alas, unbearable, addiction comes, let's turn on the lamp, grab the gun and blow into it, sucking for excitement, regardless of the fields turning to ashes, enjoying life is arranged by fate, you don't eat and you won't get rich." Although this is playful writing, it depicts the psychology of smokers vividly.

There is also a poem about people smoking, saying: "A withered skeleton ascends to the ghost register, two lines of clear tears tremble on the shoulders of the poet, and the door of the room is half-closed, resenting people asking, the curtains are low, knowing only oneself," all of which are worthy of depicting the situation.

— Deeply Immeasurable

Little Western Paradise 175

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Episode Twenty-One: Gently Complying, Over the Courtyard, Pitying the Moonlight Appearance; Vigorously Instructing the Son-in-Law, Listening to the Lion's Roar from the Next Room

As he spoke, he smiled slightly at Zhiqian again, expecting his concrete reply. Zhiqian thought for a moment and laughed: Although there is a way, I am not convenient to announce it temporarily. Bei Hai put down his hand and unconsciously stretched it to his head to scratch it a few times, asking: Not convenient to announce? Zhiqian simply gave him a conundrum to guess, smiling and nodding twice. At this moment, he had a chance to turn around and heard the servant whispering a series of words in the next room. What he was reporting was the matter of Jia Duocai and his wife in the front yard. Zhiqian looked at the wall, smiled and looked at Bei Hai, and then the two listened further. He heard the woman answer: What? Is that man named Jia bullying people like this! How much money did he spend to buy out someone else's family? The servant replied: I heard it was one hundred and fifty yuan. The woman said: One hundred and fifty yuan to break up someone else's family, this man named Jia is too cruel. But the family who sold Jia's daughter is too worthless, just one hundred and fifty yuan. The servant did not speak, there was a smile, and the director said slowly: Just one hundred and fifty yuan? Is that a small amount? In Gansu, there are many people who sell their sons and daughters for one yuan and fifty cents. The woman issued a very stern voice and said: If there are such cheap people, why don't you buy two heads for me? The director replied: That was when there was a famine two years ago. The woman said: You're talking nonsense about what happened two years ago? The director was silent. The woman said: Servant, call one of the woman's family members, I have something to say to him. The servant laughed: Mrs. Hu, why bother asking about their affairs. They are all people without knowledge, and if one sentence is not pleasant, they will start crying. The woman said: People don't shed tears unless they are sad. If they haven't been wronged, why would they cry? I'm not afraid of crying, you just call someone over, I have something important to ask him. Then there were footsteps, and the servant brought a smiling face from outside the window. (368)

Notes on What I Saw 176

— (Yangzijiang)

In an alley that runs from Jiaozhou Road to the Shen Garden football field, on the tall walls of the Meiyi Company, I saw four large white chalk characters: "Ban Che Zhaotie (禁扯招貼)." Of course, this is a misspelling of "Ban Zhi Zhaotie (禁止招貼)," which means "No Posting." But how much is it enough to make people feel the sense of "a slight deviation can lead to a great difference!"

The complexity of the construction of Chinese characters is indeed a drawback. However, the misuse of the characters "Zhi (止)" and "Che (扯)" still seems too bizarre. Just imagine, "Ban Che Zhaotie (禁扯招貼)" doesn't it not only not prohibit posting but also give posters a kind of protection?

If the owner of Meiyi Company passed by here, I think he would definitely smile.

This column is named "Notes on What I Saw" and intends to be published regularly. Readers are welcome to submit articles. — Editor

Beauty Chrysanthemum 177

— Zhu Ying

It was when chrysanthemums were in full bloom last year that a girl began to come to my dormitory to sell fresh flowers. Every day, a full basket, in less than half an hour, was always sold out, and she happily carried the empty basket back. Although the patrons were all young, hungry wolves, buying flowers was just a pretext. In reality, they were buying the girl's smile, but the girl did not hesitate to give a few unpriced smiles to promote her fresh flowers.

According to the girl, her surname was Huang, and her name was Jumei, sixteen years old, from Shantang outside Suzhou City. Because her father died, and there was a mother and younger siblings, she had to come out to earn some meager profits to make a living. So a Yangchang talented man named Lao Yu gave her a trademark called "Beauty Chrysanthemum."

Beauty Chrysanthemum, probably because the title of "Beauty" was added, was not as frost-resistant as chrysanthemum branches and often had a slight cough. Every month or half a month, she would always be sick for two or three days. Although she wore a thick layer of white powder on her face and some outdated red rouge, the back of her neck and hands showed a deep layer of ginger yellow. Therefore, our Yangchang talented man, Lao Yu, pinched his nose and recited to her, "Pitiable person is thinner than yellow flower." When Beauty Chrysanthemum heard him recite this, she always twisted her slender waist and said, "Pee, what do you want to pity me for? Really unlucky!" Following these few sentences, there was always a burst of happy laughter from a large group of young people.

From July of this year, Beauty Chrysanthemum no longer came to our dormitory. Her mother came to replace her, saying that her daughter was suffering from weakness and was lying down and could not come out. But the old woman came for a week, and no one paid attention, so she brought Beauty Chrysanthemum's twelve-year-old sister every day. Although the business was not as good as Beauty Chrysanthemum, it was still able to sell some.

Yesterday, a sad message was brought by the old woman and shook the whole dormitory, saying that Beauty Chrysanthemum had died. What a coincidence, it was the season when yellow flowers wither!

Strange Duck Egg 178

— (Ji Yijie)

The cook at the Kang Nao Tuo Road Mental Hospital in this city recently purchased several duck eggs from the local market. The shells were greenish in color (commonly called green-shelled duck eggs). Unexpectedly, upon opening them, he discovered a strange egg. The eggshell and yolk were no different from ordinary eggs, but the egg white was blood-red, which he found very peculiar. He immediately reported it to the hospital staff, who were all amazed. It is said that the hospital is now storing this egg in a glass cup, along with the eggshell, for proper preservation. This is hastily recorded for the study of physiologists.

General Mobilization of Laughter 179

— (Zhu )

It is said that a constant smile is good for one's health, as the saying goes: "A smile a day keeps the doctor away." In these times when all major matters must be discussed later, let's find a few jokes to tell. "While there's life, there's hope." If we cultivate a healthy body, what can we not do? Therefore, promoting jokes is no less effective than holding a sports meeting! Haha!

The King of Freeloaders Zhao Jun, an unemployed vagrant, relied on his robust physique to repeatedly scam food and drink in hotels and restaurants. After filling his belly, he would wipe his mouth, say hello, and those timid shopkeepers, considering themselves unlucky, would let him leave triumphantly. Some less agreeable shopkeepers, apart from giving him a beating, could only drag him to the police station. Luckily, he had a strong body; a few blows were nothing to him. Even if he was taken to the police station and detained for a few days, Zhao Jun didn't care. Once released, he would continue his ways, freeloading as he pleased. One day, Zhao Jun was dragged into the Public Security Bureau again for freeloading. The branch director, unable to bear it any longer, personally interrogated him. After asking the usual questions like his name, he asked with a smile, "Why do you keep freeloading?" Zhao Jun also smiled and said, "Director, if I don't freeload, I'll be hungry; wouldn't I starve to death?" The director still said with a smile, "Fine, if you can't live without freeloading, I'll just fulfill your wish. I'll send you to a reformatory to freeload for years!" As the director spoke, his face was still smiling, but the smile on Zhao Jun's face vanished instantly.

Amusing Anecdotes of Gamblers Three famous gamblers, A, B, and C, met one day and planned to gamble. After making arrangements, they invited Mr. D to play mahjong together. After the four of them started the game, they naturally adopted the principle of "three feeding one," using secret signals to communicate. They were gleefully "carrying Mr. D in a sedan chair" when Mr. D, who was also an experienced gambler, noticed something was amiss. He carefully observed and completely deciphered the secret signals of A, B, and C. So, when A wanted tiles of the "tube" suit, he would give A the tube tiles; when B wanted tiles of the "string" suit, he would give B the string tiles. A, B, and C were completely baffled by Mr. D, like Zhang Tianshi, the Taoist master, gazing at each other in confusion. In the end, Mr. D used his skills and won over a hundred yuan. A, B, and C looked at each other, sighed, and said to each other, "Unexpectedly, we three sedan carriers have become car engines today, getting driven around so much that we can't be our own masters!" (Note: In gambling mahjong, "three feeding one" is called "carrying the sedan chair," and "one feeding three" is called "sitting in a car.")

Eating Crab Antics In the ninth month for female crabs and the tenth month for male crabs, when the chrysanthemums are blooming, crabs are naturally a seasonal delicacy. The fat and roe are plentiful, and the taste is endless. So, in the past few days, crabs have become a good accompaniment to wine in restaurants. One day, Mr. A was drinking with his friends and said with a laugh, "These days, crabs are worth savoring, so old crabs are ultimately good things." Mr. B laughed, "Don't brag. You're the type who gets drunk even from wine dregs. Whether it's old crabs or small crabs, it's truly 'like a beggar eating a dead crab, every one is good.'" These two gentlemen were already quite drunk. Over the topic of old crabs and dead crabs, they argued back and forth, verbally sparring and exchanging insults. They smashed cups and bowls, overturned tables and benches. Mr. A's head was smashed by Mr. B, and Mr. B's mouth was punched swollen by Mr. A. The police tied them up and took them to the police station. The next day, after sobering up, A and B sighed and said to each other, "For the sake of old crabs, we became two big 'bundled crabs' last night."

Cotton Yarn: November Contracts, Cotton Yarn Delivery and its Process; Market Prices Reach New Highs from Low to High; Trading is Active and the Delivery Volume is Quite Alarming 183

Golden Rooster Brand Yarn The November contract was listed on June 1st of this year, with a price of 169.8 yuan, gradually rising to 171.9 yuan. Then, due to the unrest in the north and the deep penetration of foreign yarn into the mainland, selling at reduced prices, Chinese yarn was greatly hit. In addition, the silver market was extremely tight, business in all directions was depressed, and Japanese merchants frequently sold. On June 19th, the lowest price was seen at 165.9 yuan. At this time, the price of yarn fell daily, and the factory was in great difficulty. A part of the operation was difficult, and those who stopped or reduced work due to inflexible turnover became more serious. As production decreased, the market showed a positive trend, and as the gold bar rose, rumors spread in the market, saying that the currency problem would definitely be realized. And those close to a certain aspect rushed to the cotton yarn market and absorbed a large amount. As a result, the market moved forward, and the highest price was seen at 179.6 yuan on July 29th. Unexpectedly, after the price was high, it hindered actual sales, customers stopped working, and business felt particularly deserted. The market price went from high to low. How could one know that it would rain every night in a leaky house? The U.S. cotton loan was changed from 1.2 to 0.9, and the world cotton industry had a once crazy decline trend. The yarn market followed the trend and went down, repeatedly breaking the 70 yuan mark. Later, after October, the rising trend in the market gradually subsided, and the rumors of the gold bar market were extremely fierce. The enthusiasm of the people was rare in history. The price of gold skyrocketed, quickly breaking through three major barriers, breaking through 1,000 yuan, then to more than 100 yuan, and then rushing out of the 200 yuan barrier, with new peaks appearing one after another. The market was greatly shocked, and rumors abounded. The crowds focused on currency, and speculators were enthusiastic. The banking industry first bought frantically, and the chips in the market became more and more tight. The market soared, pushing towards the peak. On November 4th, after the Ministry of Finance announced that the banknotes of the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications were legal tender, the market became more chaotic. Later, with a certain party willing to maintain and spit out according to the market to stabilize the market. However, the frenzy of buying created a new record since the start of the exchange, with a plate soaring by 5.5 yuan, breaking through the 200 yuan barrier, and the highest peak reaching 202 yuan, the new high price since December of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Later, due to the emergence of bulls and the assassination of Japanese sailors in Hongkou, there were many doubts in the market, and rumors arose, causing prices to fall step by step, again breaking the 90 yuan barrier. Before long, public debt rose, and Shanghai dispelled rumors from the authorities, and the people were greatly relieved. Investigation: The Rise and Fall of the Financial Industry in Wuxi 195

The financial power of Wuxi has always been in the hands of money shops. The main targets of money shop loans are the silk and rice industries. During the heyday of the silk factory industry in 1929, there were a total of 56 silk factories in the county, with more than 20,000 silk machines and nearly 100,000 workers. With the development of the silk industry, the number of money shops also increased. Within two years, the number of money shops increased from ten to twenty. Loans to the silk industry were very generous. At that time, there were only a few banks in Wuxi, such as China Communications, Shanghai, and Jiangsu. The China Communications and other banks were specializing in issuing banknotes. Although Jiangsu and Shanghai also made loans for silk cocoons, the number was very small.

In 1931, the overseas silk market fell sharply. The silk factories in Wuxi had a mountain of accumulated silk and suffered huge losses. About 30 silk factories went bankrupt one after another. As a result, every money shop suffered bad debts, ranging from 12,000 to more than 100,000 yuan. The money industry suffered such a major blow, and its vitality was greatly damaged. As a result, the newly established money shops also went bankrupt one after another. Last spring, the Baokangrun Money Shop, which had strong financial resources, could not maintain itself and announced liquidation. Up to this year, there are only nine exchange money shops in the county: Ruichangrun, Fuyu, Fuyuan, Shenyu, Yonghengfeng, Yuanfengren, Deji, Fuchangsheng, and Yunyu.

Wuxi is a well-known lending port. In addition to lending in the silk market, the most important thing is lending in the rice industry. There are more than 120 large and small rice shops in the county. The amount of loans often reaches more than 10 million yuan in the summer and winter seasons. The money industry has suffered deep trauma and no longer has the ability to operate large-scale loans. At the same time, it does not dare to lend easily. Therefore, the four banks, China Communications, Shanghai, and Jiangsu, took the opportunity to lend in large quantities, because rice industry loans have goods as collateral and profits are guaranteed, so why not the banking industry? In this way, a large part of the money shops' business was taken away by the banks. Therefore, in the past three years, various banks in Shanghai have set up branches in Wuxi to issue banknotes and operate loans. Competition among peers is fierce. The three banks, China, Communications, and Jiangsu, have built their own warehouses to specialize in rice and grain loans. Now there are a total of ten banks in Wuxi: China, Communications, Jiangsu, Shanghai, Industrial, Zhejiang Xingye, Continental, Zhongnan, Farmers, and Commercial. Shanghai Xinhua Bank has set up an office in Dangkou Town in the Eighth District, specializing in rural loans. Shanghai Bank has set up a branch office in the urban area, specializing in attracting household deposits.

On the surface, Wuxi's financial industry has been replaced by the banking industry (the money industry). But what is the truth? Although the number of banks is increasing, is the business of the banks expanding proportionally? This has become a question. Wuxi's rice industry has been affected by the dumping of foreign rice and foreign wheat in recent years, and most of them have found it difficult to survive. Last winter, due to the famine, the business of each rice shop was even more desolate. Other industries such as textiles, silk cloth, and foreign goods have all declined uniformly. The targets of bank loans were so depressed last year and this year. Can the banks themselves still be prosperous?

This spring, there were huge waves in the Shanghai financial industry, and the Wuxi financial industry was also greatly affected. Banks and money shops tightened loans, and almost everyone was unwilling to operate spring cocoon loans. The released cocoon loans were only 2 million yuan, which is less than one-tenth compared to five years ago. When Qiuerdeng entered the market, the silk market soared. The silver and money industry learned from the previous lessons and still dared not lend in large quantities. It was really too steady. Now that the new rice is on the market, the banks and money shops are still adhering to a tight policy and are unwilling to lend easily. The industrial and commercial market is showing a more desolate situation. If this continues without devising an appropriate good strategy, I don't know what the future of the financial industry will be. (Jian Qing)

Talking Points

Saving the Nation Through Buddhist Ceremony 207

— Meng Ruo

The Vajra Dharma Assembly has been held twice in the past, once in Beiping and once in Hangzhou. These days, a White Umbrella Cover Pacifying Disaster Dharma Assembly is being held here, which is truly grand. It is said that the initiators, in view of the increasing demonic influence and the many misfortunes of the country, in order to eliminate the calamities, specially invited the Panchen Lama's representative, Rongzeng Master from Tibet, and Mongolian and Tibetan eminent monks to hold the Dharma Assembly for three days, hoping to rely on the power of the Buddha to escape the crisis. This is considered saving the nation through Dharma Assembly.

To solve the nation's worries, one should make efforts in a rational way to be effective. Using Dharma Assembly to salvage the misfortunes, the intention may not be criticized, but the action is inevitably eccentric. In order to correct social perceptions, it is also necessary to criticize it. It must be known that saving the nation is a difficult task, relying entirely on strength, and must not have any fluke. The behavior of seeking gods and entrusting Buddha is not what we should have. If Dharma Assembly can eliminate disasters and difficulties, it is the most powerful treasure. Our national crisis, just invite a few masters to perform the Dharma, can deal with it, what else do we need saving the nation movement?

The Vajra Dharma Assembly in the past was presided over by the Living Buddha Panchen Lama, which was not a sensation. But the result was just wasted money. Not long ago, the Pope of Rome led the world's Catholics to pray for peace for three days. In the end, it could not eliminate the massacre in East Africa.

Here, we advise the general public who are "determined to save the nation" that if you have the heart to save the nation, everyone should do their best. Otherwise, no matter how great the Dharma is, I am afraid it will not be enough to save our calamity.

Guangzhou in Winter 208

— Muxian

Winter seems to be unrelated to the southern country. For example, now, it should be the season of falling leaves and frost everywhere in the north and south of the Yangtze River. However, the grass and trees in the south are still so green and lovely, the women are still wearing cicada-winged summer clothes, and the swimming pools in Dongshan and Xijiao are relatively deserted. But there are still many young people showing off their power, and the ball-like banyan trees are still full of thick shade, arranged neatly there in the long embankment. It is the season when azaleas are in full bloom in the southern country, and the clacking sound of the nanny's wooden sandals is loud. The warm sun shines on the female students wearing blue plaid cloth skirts. Who dares to say it is winter?

Counting up, it has been eight years since I spent winter in Guangzhou. If there is no special reason this year, I believe that the opportunity to avoid the cold in the south will not be lost anyway.

The kapok on Yuexiu Mountain is probably about to bloom, right? Those bright red flowers are sparsely hanging on the thick branches, definitely not as graceful as wintersweet, and even less as delicate and beautiful as peach blossoms. The temperament is just like a Confucian general with literary grace and elegance. No wonder kapok has another alias of hero tree.

Although Lychee Bay is deserted. But those who like tranquility and quietness may as well invite three or five close friends to hire a boat to float in the middle of the stream, listening to the singing of the yellow orioles on both sides. Or stretch your neck and breathe in the fresh air unique to the suburbs? This leisurely life will bring so many romantic atmospheres!

On the streets, there are also flags of winter discounts fluttering in the wind, and lottery tickets (one type of fortune tickets) fly all over the streets like paper money. Chaozhou oranges are on the market. Those bowl-sized oranges will make your mouth water. Maybe there are one or two Liangxiang ticket shops on the most bustling road. To embellish a little, that pungent smell will make you sneeze. The radio in the foreign goods store emits that discordant Cantonese music, which makes people very impatient. There is a burst of rough gong sound in the teahouse. A stench of opium smoke may float out from a small alley, making you very sad.

The Pearl River Bridge, like a giant, spans the turbulent rapids. Ant-like pedestrians are crowded on the bridge. Many pale faces showed hurried expressions. Among them, there are naturally fewer gamblers who rush to "Fantan Halls" and addicts who go to "Talk Shops."

After crossing the bridge, the Henan Island, which is called the Monte Carlo of the East, appears in front of you. The big words of "Yutai Company Upstairs Silver Plate" first pull your footsteps tight. Batches of gamblers with slumped faces and suffering from a psychological illness of luck came out of that narrow door, and batches of people with too much hope rushed in. Although I did not mix in it, this Oriental Monte Carlo hurt my heart after all.

It will never be as desolate and cold as a winter night in the north. At midnight, you can still see the dazzling neon lights. Teahouses, restaurants, etc. are still so lively. If you are interested, you may as well go to the teahouse that hires female entertainers to sing to while away the time.

The sound of wooden clogs at midnight awakens people's dreams. The hawker selling wontons is knocking on the bamboo clapper, the sound is so clear and sharp, and there is no northwest wind raging, even if you are only wearing a single coat, you will not shiver. How lovely is the southern country! I would like to spend every winter in your arms.

Goddess 209

— Jiang Mi

That night, the stars and the moon also lost their light, and the entire universe was just a black mass. It was difficult for them to be gods in this niche again. They were going to create new light and new warmth. The five goddesses quietly disappeared on the sea behind the tower, farewell to the black universe.

The Person Who Strings Willow Leaves 210

— Luo Zhihua

When a thin layer of ice begins to form in the water tanks of the northern country, our young people have work to do.

In the rural areas of our hometown, you can see tall poplars everywhere. Poplar is a tall deciduous tree. Every spring, when it starts to sprout, it will drop a kind of "poplar grub" that looks like a caterpillar; in spring, young children use their frozen red hands to pick them up. While singing songs with other partners, they pick them into small baskets; when a small basket is full, they send it to the old grandmother who is sitting not far away from the crowd and doing living. She always takes it kindly and pours it into the prepared cloth bag. Then go back and pick again. In autumn, the willow leaves fall again, and we come to string them again.

Because the willow leaves are pieces, so big and cute, it is not appropriate to pick them up by hand, so we come to string them. The method of stringing is to use a bamboo needle (or iron needle) with a long rope strung on the tail, and a block at the end of the rope. In this way, use the needle to string the willow leaves all over the ground, string them full, put them on the rope, string them full, put them on the rope, and wait until the rope is full, then drag this long string home. Sometimes, I bring a few more ropes, and string this one full and then string that one.

When we walk into the house of the old grandmother, these things are often hung on his walls.

In order to study, I lived in the city most of the time. In autumn, spring holidays, and the "wheat holiday" specially given to older students, I lived in the countryside. I followed, in the fields, in the woods, watching those wave-like wheat, the round apricots, pears, peaches, followed by fat to thin, from thin to fat cattle, horses, and other livestock. I learned a lot of knowledge from those people that I learned in school.

But what I will never forget are those people who strung willow leaves together.

These people, now recalling them, are somewhat vague. However, when I see them, I am still very affectionate, but they have been crushed by life and no longer have the joy of the past. And the former partners, some have become mothers, some have been sold as commodities, some are still following behind the tails of cows, supporting the plow, and some have run to the city like me. What I got in the city was starvation and cold that came before death. They are suffering from salary cuts, layoffs, unemployment, ... oppression, struggling on the lifeline. Like those who are still in the fields, they are just suffering from two forms of oppression.

Some time ago, I met one of those partners. His physique was much taller than mine. In childhood, whether it was stringing willow leaves or picking up "poplar grubs," he always achieved the best results. Five years ago, he transferred home from Jilin and ran to the city again.

When the waves of the Huangpu River angrily hit the dock, he was there, he was working there "Hengyo, Hengyo."

He told me the pain of life and gave me many inspirations.

He waved his arm with the black bird's feathers on it, as if facing his partner, and said to me: "What you said is right: Can you still endure hardship for a lifetime?..." When his arm was raised, I seemed to see the sea waves that were about to destroy this world, rushing towards the rocks of the world.

He said, "There are many people who string willow leaves." Then he told me who had died and who had been shot by whom there. He was very clear. He could tell me those difficult-to-remember years and days. It was as if his brain was full of things about his partners.

Now, it is time to string willow leaves again, but I am wandering in a foreign country thousands of miles away, expressing infinite respect to this former partner on the one hand, and missing those who were more official on the other hand.
