Life 211

— Jiyi

Once it gets dark, the west wind blows loudly, and people in thin jackets can't help but shiver. The wind howls past in the gaps between the wires in the air, and sparse pedestrians tap the streets unevenly with their feet: "Tap, tap, tap...", in the distance, the street lights gradually become denser, and the machines in the factory spit the sound of breathing out, rising and falling vaguely and rhythmically.

A thin and strangely shaped shadow is projected on the deserted street by the street lamp in front. Wang Dagezi, with a feverish brain and a tongue dulled by being soaked in shochu, walks crookedly along the "foreign-style houses" by the road. Then, suddenly, he stops at a narrow doorway and pounds on the door hurriedly and violently.

"Ah Lin, open the door, Ah Lin, open the door! Damn you..."

Unclear, acid-smelling shochu-flavored words spew out like pouring, and then, with a snap, the small door opens, and a tall body blocks the door, filling the door frame.

"Who?... You? What do you want? What do you want!"

"What do I want? Don't be kidding, right? The money you lost in the gambling den the other day, are you still planning to pay it back? You say! Tell me honestly!"

"Speak a little clearer! What gambling den are you talking about?"

"Hum, hum, hum" Wang Dagezi squeezed a string of terrible sounds from his throat: "Friend... Boss, don't be kidding, right? Three yuan and four cents, won in your gambling den! Waiting to live a life! You also lost a lot in your gambling den, Boss, didn't you?" (To be continued)

Misty Fine Vistas 212

— Fang Zhou

The Misty Peak is shrouded in milky white morning mist, and the rising sun is reflected on the mountain peak, faintly revealing a blurred outline. Looking up from the Zhenxia Harbor, it is as if a young woman with newly applied rouge stands under a piece of blue satin; the sun gradually rises, and the golden color slowly fades.

Junping and I sat separately in two rickshaws and headed towards Luohan Weir; but the high and low, rugged mountain roads shook us sitting in the cars so much that our hearts almost turned over. Sometimes, when passing between rice paddies, or beside ponds, or streams, we would feel a burst of fear in our hearts, fearing that the car and people would fall into the rice paddies and ponds together.

With a uneasy heart, the car turned a few corners, and after passing Shangjian Bridge, we could see a Wenchang Pavilion.

Tung seeds fell from the tree with a crackling sound, and the leaves all turned withered yellow, and only a few withered leaves were flying in the air. The dilapidated Wenchang Pavilion has now been converted into a private primary school, and the open space in front of the door is probably the primary school's playground.

After walking a few more steps, the car could no longer be pulled in. We gave the car fare and walked along a stone path overgrown with short pine trees. Leather shoes rubbed against the sand, making a crackling sound. The weather in late autumn was so sunny and mild that after running a few steps, I felt hot all over; the sweat on my forehead was dripping like water leaking from the eaves. I took off my woolen hat and wiped the sweat with a handkerchief.

"It's really hot!" I stood and exhaled a sigh of relief, Junping just smiled and said nothing.

We squatted under a bayberry tree to rest, and a breeze brought a bit of light coolness. The clear and loud sound of a waterfall was sent out from the nearby valley, so we followed the sound and looked for it in a small path of chestnut trees. Walking along a small stream for more than ten steps, we saw two huge stone slabs, and the waterfall, which was like a piece of silk and hung upside down like a silver river, rushed straight down from above, and then was received by the stone slabs below into a clear and deep pool, stirring up water flowers like broken silver. The water was so clear and lovely that the pebbles at the bottom of the stream could be counted one by one.

"That is the Battle Stone Slab. The sound of the waterfall here in the plum season is like thunder." I held the rushing waterfall with my hands, and the water droplets splashed on my face.

Junping took off his shoes and socks, wanting to soak his feet in this clear spring, but the water was too cold, so he quickly retracted his feet as soon as he stretched them down: "Too cold, can't stand it!"

There are many stone gaps left on the stone slabs next to it, and there is still charcoal ash in the gaps; that is the traces of tourists coming here to cook spring water and drink tea.

Several country women were squatting in the thatch bushes on the hillside of Zhuwu Ridge, cutting firewood. When they heard our leather shoes, they stopped working and stood up at the same time, looking at us with suspicious eyes.

The soles of our leather shoes stepped on the winding brick mountain road, and there was often the danger of slipping. We could only stoop our waists and climb upwards. When we climbed to the highest peak of Zhuwu Ridge, both of us were panting, sweating profusely. Looking up at the top of the Misty Peak, it was still half as high.

There was a narrow path to the west, winding straight upwards. We wiped the sweat from our faces, stretched our waists, and continued to climb upwards from that path.

There is a teahouse on the top of Misty Peak, with a stone-carved tea jar inside, which Hao is used by the villagers to provide tea in summer. Because this is the only way to go north and south of the mountain, there are many people who come and go every day, and that teahouse is the only resting place for pedestrians. This is truly an oasis in the desert in summer.

Standing on the top of the peak and looking around, you can overlook the entire Taihu Lake scenery. 36,000 hectares of vastness, 72 strange peaks of Dongting, all the lake and mountain scenery are taken into view, and the outlines of two provinces and three prefectures rise and fall in the sparkling waves of thousands of miles.

Don't be in love with the fragrance of wild flowers, wild flowers are not as fragrant as home flowers.

Suzhou Ballad Singing 216

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Dun Ben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening Chapter "Sudden Change"

The sky is clear, the wind is light, and the air is refreshing. A few lines of new geese fly across the sky. The busy servant Gao Lishi sweeps the imperial garden with great effort. The autumn scenery in the inner garden is endless. Lotus leaves are everywhere in the ponds. Soon, it is reported that Emperor Ming has arrived, with the favored Consort Yang supported on either side. Countless osmanthus flowers are fragrant. Sometimes parrots call to each other. The imperial banquet is laid out on the flower pavilion. Delicacies from the sea and mountains fill the table.

A jade hand holds a golden pot. The emperor taps the beat, the consort sings. The Rainbow Skirt Dance is unparalleled in the world. Consort Yang kneels and presents three cups of wine. The emperor happily holds her hand. Consort Yang falls drunk, like a painting of a begonia in spring slumber. Her drunken state is even more enchanting. Who knew that joy would turn to sorrow. It is said that An Lushan's rebellion is in full swing. What can be done about the capital? The Tang Dynasty has been at peace for too long. The civil and military officials are unable to defend against the enemy. The six armies are quickly ordered to protect the emperor. The carriages and horses rush along the long road. Temporarily avoiding the flames of war, they are lucky to go to Shu. Alas, the woman is as delicate as a flower. Her jade is shattered, her fragrance extinguished, a piece of silk. She is forced to commit suicide at Mawei Slope.

Joint Film News 221

(1) "Sea Hawk" Released

"Sea Hawk" (Drake of England), released today at the Cathay Grand Theater, is a magnificent historical naval battle film, narrating a page of miracles of the British national hero Drake in the late sixteenth century. Drake rose from a pirate to become a British naval admiral. The ministers in the court were all against his combat plan, but only Queen Elizabeth could deeply understand his ideas. Later, Drake indeed defeated the Spanish army and added a glorious page to the history of the British navy in Europe. There is a fire attack scene in the film, in which the burning ship rushes into the enemy fleet with the momentum of the wind, which is extremely shocking.

(2) "Here's To Romance" is a Box Office Success

"Here's To Romance", starring the opera master of the contemporary era, Nino Martini, has been extremely crowded since its premiere at the Grand Cathay Theater the day before yesterday. This is because the plot of the film is not only lingering and poignant, but Martini's singing voice is indeed divine, with a roundabout and lingering taste. There is also the "Swan Dance" starring the dance star Maria and the Gypsy dance by the Spanish dance king Ascortai Lu, which are not easy to see on the screen and are worth watching.

(3) "Wings Over Ethiopia" is Coming Soon

At this time when the situation in Ethiopia is extremely tense, this movie screen "Wings Over Ethiopia" is bound to be worth our attention. In this film, it thoroughly exposes the customs of Ethiopia. King Haile Selassie is no less than the protagonist of the film. The exercise of the latest tactics by the Lion King's army and the air defense equipment of Ethiopia are all reflected on the screen, which is a refreshing experience for the audience. It is said that this film will be released soon at the Grand Cathay.

(4) "The 39 Steps" Arrives in Shanghai

The big star Robert Donat has gained great fame since the release of "The Count of Monte Cristo", but so far there have been no new works released, and there are quite a few fans who are eagerly awaiting him. Now, his new work "The 39 Steps" has arrived in Shanghai and will be released in Shanghai soon. In this film, not only is the structure ingenious everywhere, but Robert Donat's acting skills are even better than in "The Count of Monte Cristo". It is indeed a rare work to see. The heroine is Marlene Carroll, the protagonist of "Rose Marie" and "The Scarlet Empress", and the director of this film is Hitchcock, the director of "The Lodger".

"Hero of the Hour" to be Released Soon 222

Yi Hua Company's latest and most valuable production, the all-dialogue sound singing film "Hero of the Hour", under the clamor of the world, has decided to meet the audiences who support it in the first-class theaters in this city and other cities in the near future. Regarding the organization of this film, and other aspects, director Ying Yunwei already has the ambition to show it to the foreign film fans, so there is no doubt that he has achieved satisfactory results. At the same time, the day of its release can resonate for a while, and give the Chinese film industry a fierce impulse and fresh stimulation, which is also expected.
